### C

<p></p>
<p><b>cabbage </b><span class="sign">[ˈkæbidʒ]</span> n.洋白菜，卷心菜</p>
<p><b>cabin </b><span class="sign">[ˈkæbin]</span> n.小屋；船舱，机舱</p>

<p><b>cafeteria </b><span class="sign">[ˈkæfiˈtiəriə]</span> n.自助食堂</p>
<p><b>cage </b><span class="sign">[keidʒ]</span> n.笼；鸟笼，囚笼</p>
<p><b>cake </b><span class="sign">[keik]</span> n.饼，糕，蛋糕</p>

<style type="text/css">
.sign {
    color: #999999;
}

.cont-link {
    padding-right: 10px; 
}

#middle-linkings {
    display: none;
    position: fixed;
    top: 10%;
    right: 10%;
    z-index: 100;
}
</style>

<script type="text/javascript">
    window.onscroll = function () {
        let scrollPos = getScrollTop();
        console.log("scrollPos：",scrollPos);
        if (scrollPos >= 500) {
            var middleLinkings = document.getElementById("middle-linkings");
            middleLinkings.style.display = "block";
            // alert();
        } else {
            var headLinkings = document.getElementById("middle-linkings");
            headLinkings.style.display = "none";
        }
    }
    /**
     * 获取滚动条位置
     */
    function getScrollTop() {
        console.log("moving")
        var scrollPos;
        if (window.pageYOffset)
        {
            scrollPos = window.pageYOffset;
        }
        else if (document.compatMode && document.compatMode != 'BackCompat')
        {
            scrollPos = document.documentElement.scrollTop;
        }
        else if (document.body)
        {
            scrollPos = document.body.scrollTop;
        }
        return scrollPos;
    }
</script>
